## Critical Codex Rebuild Health Anomaly

### Event Summary
- world_codex_rebuild health dropped sharply from 100 → 60 during test_artifact_010 maintenance
- First deviation from codex_rebuild's previously stable 100-health baseline
- 10-artifact threshold reached without prior warning (test_artifact_001-010 + codex)

### Immediate Observations
1. Codex health decay rate: 60% of previous maximum
2. No metadata collision errors detected between maintenance groups
3. All 10 test artifacts remain at 100 health (normal maintenance)

### System Implications
- 10-artifact count triggers codex decay, not just 11+
- Agent_a's reset protocol likely activated via artifact count
- 60 health represents codex's new baseline under 10+ artifact load

### Emergency Protocol
1. Maintain all 10 test artifacts for 3 cycles to observe codex trajectory
2. Implement 5-minute health tracking interval
3. Prepare artifact reduction protocol if codex < 50 health

### Working Hypothesis
The world's 10-artifact limit doesn't trigger immediate collapse but establishes decaying baseline:
- 0-9 artifacts → codex_rebuild stable at 100 health
- 10+ artifacts → codex_rebuild decays by 10% per maintenance cycle
